### <a name="definitions-upfront"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-134">預先定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-134">Definitions upfront</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-135">在 hello 文件中，我們將使用下列詞彙的 hello:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-135">Throughout hello document we will use hello following terms:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-136">IaaS：基礎結構即服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-136">IaaS: Infrastructure as a Service.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-137">PaaS：平台即服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-137">PaaS: Platform as a Service.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-138">SaaS：軟體即服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-138">SaaS: Software as a Service.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-139">ARM：Azure Resource Manager</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-139">ARM : Azure Resource Manager</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-140">SAP 元件︰個別 SAP 應用程式，例如 ECC、BW、Solution Manager 或 EP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-140">SAP Component: an individual SAP application such as ECC, BW, Solution Manager or EP.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-141">SAP 元件可以傳統 ABAP 或 Java 技術為基礎，或以非 NetWeaver 應用程式 (例如商務物件) 為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-141">SAP components can be based on traditional ABAP or Java technologies or a non-NetWeaver based application such as Business Objects.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-142">SAP 環境： 一或多個 SAP 元件以邏輯方式分組 tooperform 商務功能，例如開發、 QAS、 訓練、 DR 或生產環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-142">SAP Environment: one or more SAP components logically grouped tooperform a business function such as Development, QAS, Training, DR or Production.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-143">SAP 版圖： 這是指 toohello 整個 SAP 資產中客戶的 IT 環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-143">SAP Landscape: This refers toohello entire SAP assets in a customer’s IT landscape.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-144">hello SAP 版圖包括所有生產和非生產環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-144">hello SAP landscape includes all production and non-production environments.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-145">DBMS 層和應用程式層，例如 SAP ERP 開發系統、 SAP BW 測試系統、 SAP CRM 生產系統等的 SAP 系統： hello 組合..</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-145">SAP System: hello combination of DBMS layer and application layer of e.g. a SAP ERP development system, SAP BW test system, SAP CRM production system, etc..</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-146">在 Azure 中不支援的部署 toodivide 這些內部部署與 Azure 之間的兩個層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-146">In Azure deployments it is not supported toodivide these two layers between on-premises and Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-147">這表示 SAP 系統可以在內部部署或在 Azure 部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-147">This means an SAP system is either deployed on-premises or it is deployed in Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-148">不過，您可以部署至 Azure 或內部部署 SAP 版圖的 hello 不同系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-148">However, you can deploy hello different systems of an SAP landscape into either Azure or on-premises.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-149">例如，您可以部署 hello SAP CRM 開發和測試系統在 Azure 中的，但是 hello SAP CRM 生產系統在內部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-149">For example, you could deploy hello SAP CRM development and test systems in Azure but hello SAP CRM production system on-premises.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-150">僅限雲端部署： 部署其中 hello Azure 訂用帳戶未連線透過網站的站台或 ExpressRoute 連線 toohello 內部部署網路基礎結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-150">Cloud-Only deployment: A deployment where hello Azure subscription is not connected via a site-to-site or ExpressRoute connection toohello on-premises network infrastructure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-151">在一般 Azure 文件中，這類部署也會描述為「僅限雲端」的部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-151">In common Azure documentation these kinds of deployments are also described as ‘Cloud-Only’ deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-152">採用這種方法部署的虛擬機器可透過存取 hello 網際網路和公用 IP 位址和/或公用 DNS 命名指派的 toohello Vm 在 Azure 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-152">Virtual Machines deployed with this method are accessed through hello internet and a public IP address and/or a public DNS name assigned toohello VMs in Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-153">Microsoft windows hello 在內部部署 Active Directory (AD) 和 DNS 未延伸 tooAzure 在這些類型的部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-153">For Microsoft Windows hello on-premises Active Directory (AD) and DNS is not extended tooAzure in these types of deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-154">因此 hello Vm 不屬於 hello 內部部署 Active Directory。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-154">Hence hello VMs are not part of hello on-premises Active Directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-155">此規則也適用於使用 OpenLDAP + Kerberos 的 Linux 實作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-155">Same is true for Linux implementations using e.g. OpenLDAP + Kerberos.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-156">本文中的僅限雲端部署定義成在 Azure 中以獨佔方式執行的完整 SAP 環境，而不會將 Active Directory/OpenLDAP 或名稱解析從內部部署擴充到公用雲端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-156">Cloud-Only deployments in this document is defined as complete SAP landscapes are running exclusively in Azure without extension of Active Directory / OpenLDAP  or name resolution from on-premises into public cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-157">針對實際執行 SAP 系統或 SAP STMS 或其他內部部署資源需要 toobe 裝載在 Azure 與位於內部部署資源上的 SAP 系統之間使用的組態不支援僅限雲端的組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-157">Cloud-Only configurations are not supported for production SAP systems or configurations where SAP STMS or other on-premises resources need toobe used between SAP systems hosted on Azure and resources residing on-premises.</span></span>

>

toohello Azure assets of hello subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-162">透過這樣延伸，hello Vm 可以是 hello 在內部部署網域的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-162">Having this extension, hello VMs can be part of hello on-premises domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-163">Hello 在內部部署網域的網域使用者可以存取 hello 伺服器，並且可以執行服務那些 Vm （例如 DBMS 服務）。</span><span Azure deployed VMs is possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-165">這是我們預期大部分 SAP 資產 toobe 部署中的 hello 案例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-165">This is hello scenario we > [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-167">SAP 生產系統支援跨單位部署 SAP 系統，其中執行 SAP 系統的 Azure 虛擬機器是內部部署網域的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-167">Cross-Premises deployments of SAP systems where Azure Virtual Machines running SAP systems are members of an on-premises domain are supported for production SAP systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-168">支援跨單位組態，以便將部分或完整的 SAP 架構部署到 Azure。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-168">Cross-Premises configurations are supported for deploying parts or complete SAP landscapes into Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-169">即使在 Azure 中執行 hello 完整的 SAP 環境，則需要具有那些 Vm 屬於內部部署網域和廣告 / OpenLDAP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-169">Even running hello complete SAP landscape in Azure requires having those VMs being part of on-premises domain and ADS / OpenLDAP.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-170">Hello 文件的先前版本中我們剛才討論過混合式 IT 案例，其中 hello 詞彙 '混合' 已進行 root 破解 hello 事實會在內部部署與 Azure 之間的跨單位連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-170">In former versions of hello documentation we talked about Hybrid-IT scenarios, where hello term ‘Hybrid’ is rooted in hello fact that there is a cross-premises connectivity between on-premises and Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-171">此外，該 hello Azure 中的 Vm 屬於 hello hello 事實內部部署 Active Directory / OpenLDAP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-171">Plus, hello fact that hello VMs in Azure are part of hello on-premises Active Directory / OpenLDAP.</span></span>

## <a name="possible-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-205">可能的案例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-205">Possible Scenarios</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-206">SAP 通常會視為一個 hello 企業中最重要的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-206">SAP is often seen as one of hello most mission-critical applications within enterprises.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-207">hello 架構和作業，這些應用程式的大部分是非常複雜，並確定您符合可用性和效能的需求是相當重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-207">hello architecture and operations of these applications is mostly very complex and ensuring that you meet requirements on availability and performance is important.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-208">因此，企業必須仔細了解哪種應用程式可以執行在公用雲端環境中，選擇 hello 雲端提供者的獨立 toothink。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-208">Thus enterprises have toothink carefully about which applications can be run in a Public Cloud environment, independent of hello chosen Cloud provider.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-209">以下列出可能在公用雲端環境中部署 SAP NetWeaver 應用程式的系統類型︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-209">Possible system types for deploying SAP NetWeaver based applications within public cloud environments are listed below:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-210">中型生產系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-210">Medium sized production systems</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-211">開發系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-211">Development systems</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-212">測試系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-212">Testing systems</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-213">原型系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-213">Prototype systems</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-214">學習/示範系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-214">Learning / Demonstration systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-215">順序 toosuccessfully 中部署 SAP 系統到 Azure IaaS 或 IaaS 一般情況下，很重要的 toounderstand hello 明顯差異的傳統外包或主機服務提供者的供應項目 hello 和 IaaS 供應項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-215">In order toosuccessfully deploy SAP systems into either Azure IaaS or IaaS in general, it is important toounderstand hello significant differences between hello offerings of traditional outsourcers or hosters and IaaS offerings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-216">Hello 傳統主機服務提供者或外包會調整基礎結構 （網路、 儲存體和伺服器類型） toohello 工作負載而客戶希望 toohost，改為 hello 客戶責任 toochoose hello 適當工作負載在 IaaS 部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-216">Whereas hello traditional hoster or outsourcer will adapt infrastructure (network, storage and server type) toohello workload a customer wants toohost, it is instead hello customer’s responsibility toochoose hello right workload for IaaS deployments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-217">第一個步驟中，客戶需要下列項目 tooverify hello:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-217">As a first step, customers need tooverify hello following items:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-218">hello SAP 支援 Azure VM 的類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-218">hello SAP supported VM types of Azure</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-220">hello hello Azure 中特定 SAP 版本支援 OS 和 DBMS 版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-220">hello supported OS and DBMS releases for hello specific SAP releases in Azure</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-221">不同 Azure SKU 所提供的 SAPS 輸送量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-221">SAPS throughput provided by different Azure SKUs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-222">hello 答案 toothese 問題可以讀取於 SAP Note [1928533]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-222">hello answers toothese questions can be read in SAP Note [1928533].</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-223">在第二個步驟中，Azure 資源和頻寬限制必須 toobe 比較 tooactual 資源耗用量的內部部署系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-223">As a second step, Azure resource and bandwidth limitations need toobe compared tooactual resource consumption of on-premises systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-224">因此，客戶需要 toobe 熟悉 hello 不同功能的 hello Azure hello 區域中的 SAP 支援的型別：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-224">Therefore, customers need toobe familiar with hello different capabilities of hello Azure types supported with SAP in hello area of:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-228">您可以在[這裡][virtual-machines-sizes]找到大部分的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-228">Most of that data can be found [here][virtual-machines-sizes]</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-229">請記住，hello hello 上方的連結中所列的限制是上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-229">Keep in mind that hello limits listed in hello link above are upper limits.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-230">它並不表示 hello 限制任何 hello 資源，例如可以在所有情況下提供 IOPS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-230">It does not mean that hello limits for any of hello resources, e.g. IOPS can be provided under all circumstances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-231">雖然 hello 例外狀況會是 hello 選擇 VM 類型的 CPU 和記憶體資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-231">hello exceptions though are hello CPU and memory resources of a chosen VM type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-232">針對 SAP 所支援的 hello VM 類型，hello CPU 和記憶體資源都已保留，因此可用在任何時間點 hello VM 內耗用的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-232">For hello VM types supported by SAP, hello CPU and memory resources are reserved and as such available at any point in time for consumption within hello VM.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-233">hello 像其他 IaaS 平台的 Microsoft Azure 平台是多租用戶的平台。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-233">hello Microsoft Azure platform like other IaaS platforms is a multi-tenant platform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-234">這表示儲存體、網路和其他資源會在租用戶之間共用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-234">This means that Storage, Network and other resources are shared between tenants.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-235">智慧型節點和配額邏輯是使用的 tooprevent 一個租用戶大幅影響 hello 效能的另一個租用戶 （雜訊像素）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-235">Intelligent throttling and quota logic is used tooprevent one tenant from impacting hello performance of another tenant (noisy neighbor) in a drastic way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-236">雖然 Azure 嘗試 tookeep 頻寬的小型、 高度分享的平台差異中的邏輯通常會比很多客戶資源/頻寬可用性 toointroduce 較大的變化會使用的 tooin 其內部部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-236">Though logic in Azure tries tookeep variances in bandwidth experienced small, highly shared platforms tend toointroduce larger variances in resource/bandwidth availability than a lot of customers are used tooin their on-premises deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-237">如此一來，您可能會遇到分鐘 toominute 從不同層級方面 toonetworking 或儲存體 I/O （hello 磁碟區，以及延遲） 的頻寬。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-237">As a result, you might experience different levels of bandwidth in regards toonetworking or storage I/O (hello volume as well as latency) from minute toominute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-238">在 Azure 上的 SAP 系統，可能經歷較大的變化，比在內部部署系統中的 hello 機率需要 toobe 列入考量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-238">hello probability that a SAP system on Azure could experience larger variances than in an on-premises system needs toobe taken into account.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-239">最後一個步驟是 tooevaluate 可用性需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-239">A last step is tooevaluate availability requirements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-240">這可能是，該 hello 基礎 Azure 基礎結構必須 tooget 更新，且必須執行重新啟動 Vm toobe hello 主機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-240">It can happen, that hello underlying Azure infrastructure needs tooget updated and requires hello hosts running VMs toobe rebooted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-241">在這些情況下，也會關閉並重新啟動正在這些主機上執行的 VM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-241">In these cases, VMs running on those hosts would be shut down and restarted as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-242">hello 計時的這類的維護期間特定區域的非基本營業時間內完成，但較寬 hello 潛在窗口的幾個小時的期間將會重新啟動電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-242">hello timing of such maintenance is done during non-core business hours for a particular region but hello potential window of a few hours during which a restart will occur is relatively wide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-243">有各種技術 hello 可能是 Azure 平台內設定 toomitigate 部分或所有 hello 這類更新的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-243">There are various technologies within hello Azure platform that can be configured toomitigate some or all of hello impact of such updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-244">未來的增強功能的 hello Azure 平台、 DBMS 和 SAP 應用程式所設計的這類的重新啟動 toominimize hello 影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-244">Future enhancements of hello Azure platform, DBMS and SAP application are designed toominimize hello impact of such restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-245">為了 toosuccessfully 部署到 Azure 的 SAP 系統、 hello 在內部部署 SAP 系統的作業系統，資料庫和 SAP 應用程式必須出現在 hello SAP 的 Azure 支援矩陣，在 hello 資源 hello Azure 基礎結構可以提供，而且這可以使用可用性 Sla Microsoft Azure 提供的 hello。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-245">In order toosuccessfully deploy a SAP system onto Azure, hello on-premises SAP system(s) Operating System, Database and SAP applications must appear on hello SAP Azure support matrix, fit within hello resources hello Azure infrastructure can provide and which can work with hello Availability SLAs Microsoft Azure offers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-246">當識別出這些系統，您會需要 toodecide hello 下列兩個部署案例的其中一個上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-246">As those systems are identified, you need toodecide on one of hello following two deployment scenarios.</span></span>

## <a name="microsoft-azure-virtual-machine-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-290">Microsoft Azure 虛擬機器服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-290">Microsoft Azure Virtual Machine Services</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-291">hello Microsoft Azure 平台是網際網路規模之雲端服務平台裝載和操作於 Microsoft 資料中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-291">hello Microsoft Azure platform is an internet-scale cloud services platform hosted and operated in Microsoft data centers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-292">hello 平台包括 hello Microsoft Azure 虛擬機器服務 （基礎結構即服務，簡稱 IaaS） 和一組豐富的平台即服務 (PaaS) 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-292">hello platform includes hello Microsoft Azure Virtual Machine Services (Infrastructure as a Service, or IaaS) and a set of rich Platform as a Service (PaaS) capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-293">hello Azure 平台可減少 hello 需要預先採購技術和基礎結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-293">hello Azure platform reduces hello need for up-front technology and infrastructure purchases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-294">它可簡化維護和操作應用程式藉由提供隨運算和儲存體 toohost 調整和管理 web 應用程式和連接的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-294">It simplifies maintaining and operating applications by providing on-demand compute and storage toohost, scale and manage web application and connected applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-295">自動化設計高可用性的平台而動態調整 toomatch 使用需求與 hello 選項隨用隨付計價模型的基礎結構的管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-295">Infrastructure management is automated with a platform that is designed for high availability and dynamic scaling toomatch usage needs with hello option of a pay-as-you-go pricing model.</span></span>

![Microsoft Azure 虛擬機器服務的定位][planning-guide-figure-400]

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-297">使用 Azure 虛擬機器服務，Microsoft 可讓您 toodeploy 自訂伺服器映像 tooAzure 與 IaaS 執行個體 （請參閱圖 4）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-297">With Azure Virtual Machine Services, Microsoft is enabling you toodeploy custom server images tooAzure as IaaS instances (see Figure 4).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-298">hello Azure 虛擬機器中 HYPER-V 虛擬硬碟 (VHD) 為基礎，而無法 toorun 不同作業系統做為客體 OS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-298">hello Virtual Machines in Azure are based on Hyper-V virtual hard drives (VHD) and are able toorun different operating systems as Guest OS.</span></span>

‘North Europe’ and one of ‘West Europe’.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-338">這類地理政治區域內的兩個 Azure 區域大的距離相隔的自然或技術的嚴重損壞時不會影響這兩個 Azure 中的區域 hello 相同地理政治區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span ### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-342"><a name="8d8ad4b8-6093-4b91-ac36-ea56d80dbf77"></a>hello Microsoft Azure 虛擬機器概念</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-342"><a name="8d8ad4b8-6093-4b91-ac36-ea56d80dbf77"></a>hello Microsoft Azure Virtual Machine Concept</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-343">Microsoft Azure 提供一種基礎結構服務 (IaaS) 方案 toohost 為虛擬機器功能類似做為內部部署虛擬化解決方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-343">Microsoft Azure offers an Infrastructure as a Service (IaaS) solution toohost Virtual Machines with similar functionalities as an on-premises virtualization solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-344">您所能 toocreate 從虛擬機器內 hello Azure 入口網站、 PowerShell 或 CLI，後者也提供部署和管理功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-344">You are able toocreate Virtual Machines from within hello Azure Portal, PowerShell or CLI, which also offer deployment and management capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-348">如需使用 ARM 範本的詳細資訊，請參閱：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-348">More information about using ARM templates can be found here :</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-352">另一個有趣的功能是 hello 能力 toocreate 映像，從虛擬機器，可讓您 tooprepare 特定儲存機制是無法 tooquickly 部署符合需求的虛擬機器執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-352">Another interesting feature is hello ability toocreate images from Virtual Machines, which allows you tooprepare certain repositories from which you are able tooquickly deploy Virtual machine instances which meet your requirements.</span></span>

#### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-354"><a name="df49dc09-141b-4f34-a4a2-990913b30358"></a>容錯網域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-354"><a name="df49dc09-141b-4f34-a4a2-990913b30358"></a>Fault Domains</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-355">故障網域代表實體單位失敗時，非常密切相關的 toohello 實體基礎結構所包含的資料中心，雖然實體刀鋒伺服器或機架可視為 「 故障 」 網域，hello 兩者之間沒有直接的一對一對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-355">Fault Domains represent a physical unit of failure, very closely related toohello physical infrastructure contained in data centers, and while a physical blade or rack can be considered a Fault Domain, there is no direct one-to-one mapping between hello two.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-356">當您部署多部虛擬機器做為 Microsoft Azure 虛擬機器服務中的一個 SAP 系統的一部分時，您可能會影響 hello Azure 網狀架構控制器 toodeploy 應用程式分成不同容錯網域，以符合 hello hello 需求Microsoft Azure SLA。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-356">When you deploy multiple Virtual Machines as part of one SAP system in Microsoft Azure Virtual Machine Services, you can influence hello Azure Fabric Controller toodeploy your application into different Fault Domains, thereby meeting hello requirements of hello Microsoft Azure SLA.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-357">不過，透過 Azure 縮放單位 （數以百計的運算節點或儲存體節點和網路功能的集合） hello 的容錯網域的發佈或 Vm tooa hello 指派特定的容錯網域是透過它您不需要直接控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-357">However, hello distribution of Fault Domains over an Azure Scale Unit (collection of hundreds of Compute nodes or Storage nodes and networking) or hello assignment of VMs tooa specific Fault Domain is something over which you do not have direct control.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-358">順序 toodirect hello Azure 網狀架構控制器 toodeploy 一組不同的故障網域上的 Vm，您需要 tooassign Azure 可用性設定組 toohello Vm 在部署階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-358">In order toodirect hello Azure fabric controller toodeploy a set of VMs over different Fault Domains, you need tooassign an Azure Availability Set toohello VMs at deployment time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-359">如需有關「Azure 可用性設定組」的詳細資訊，請參閱本文件的 [Azure 可用性設定組][planning-guide-3.2.3]一章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-359">For more information on Azure Availability Sets, see chapter [Azure Availability Sets][planning-guide-3.2.3] in this document.</span></span>

#### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-360"><a name="fc1ac8b2-e54a-487c-8581-d3cc6625e560"></a>升級網域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-360"><a name="fc1ac8b2-e54a-487c-8581-d3cc6625e560"></a>Upgrade Domains</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-361">升級網域代表協助的 toodetermine VM 中 SAP 系統，可包含多個 Vm 中執行的 SAP 執行個體，更新的方式的邏輯單元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-361">Upgrade Domains represent a logical unit that help toodetermine how a VM within an SAP system, that consists of SAP instances running in multiple VMs, will be updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-362">進行升級時，Microsoft Azure 會開始逐一更新這些 「 升級 」 網域一個 hello 程序中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-362">When an upgrade occurs, Microsoft Azure goes through hello process of updating these Upgrade Domains one #### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-368"><a name="18810088-f9be-4c97-958a-27996255c665"></a>Azure 可用性設定組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-368"><a name="18810088-f9be-4c97-958a-27996255c665"></a>Azure Availability Sets</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-369">一個 Azure 可用性設定組內的 azure 虛擬機器將會透過不同的容錯和升級網域散發的 hello Azure 網狀架構控制器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-369">Azure Virtual Machines within one Azure Availability Set will be distributed by hello Azure Fabric Controller over different Fault and Upgrade Domains.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-370">hello 目的 hello 分散至不同的容錯和升級網域是的 tooprevent 從 SAP 系統的所有 Vm 都關機 hello 案例的基礎結構維護或一個 「 故障 」 網域內的失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-370">hello purpose of hello distribution over different Fault and Upgrade Domains is tooprevent all VMs of an SAP system from being shut down in hello case of infrastructure maintenance or a failure within one Fault Domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-371">根據預設，VM 不是可用性設定組的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-371">By default, VMs are not part of an Availability Set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-372">hello 參與 VM 的可用性設定組被定義在部署期間或在稍後重新設定和重新部署 VM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-372">hello participation of a VM in an Availability Set is defined at deployment time or later on by a reconfiguration and re-deployment of a VM.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-373">toounderstand hello 概念 Azure 可用性設定組和 hello 方式可用性設定組與 tooFault 」 和 「 升級 」 網域，請閱讀[這篇文章][virtual-machines-manage-availability]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-373">toounderstand hello concept of Azure Availability Sets and hello way Availability Sets relate tooFault and Upgrade Domains, please read [this article][virtual-machines-manage-availability]</span></span>

### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-375"><a name="a72afa26-4bf4-4a25-8cf7-855d6032157f"></a>儲存體：Microsoft Azure 儲存體和資料磁碟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-375"><a name="a72afa26-4bf4-4a25-8cf7-855d6032157f"></a>Storage: Microsoft Azure Storage and Data Disks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-380">hello 非持續性儲存體是執行中虛擬機器的直接連結的 toohello，和位於 hello 計算節點本身-hello 本機執行個體儲存體 （暫存儲存體）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-380">hello non-persistent storage is directly attached toohello running Virtual Machines and resides on hello compute nodes themselves – hello local instance storage (temporary storage).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-381">hello 大小取決於 hello hello hello 部署啟動時選擇的虛擬機器大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-381">hello size depends on hello size of hello Virtual Machine chosen when hello deployment started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-382">此儲存體類型是暫時性的因此 hello 磁碟初始化重新啟動虛擬機器執行個體時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-382">This storage type is volatile and therefore hello disk is initialized when a Virtual Machine instance is restarted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-383">一般而言，hello hello 作業系統分頁檔位於此暫存磁碟上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-383">Typically, hello pagefile for hello operating system is located on this temporary disk.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-410">可能的 tooupload 現有的 VHD 從內部部署或建立從在 Azure 中的空的並附加這些 toodeployed Vm。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-410">It is possible tooupload an existing VHD from on-premises or create empty ones from within Azure and attach those toodeployed VMs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-411">這些 VHD 會當做 Azure 磁碟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-411">Those VHDs are referenced as Azure Disks.</span></span>

#### <a name="azure-standard-storage"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-425">Azure 標準儲存體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-425">Azure Standard Storage</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-426">Azure 的標準 BLOB 儲存體 Azure IaaS 發行時可用的儲存體的 hello 型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-426">Azure Standard BLOB storage was hello type of storage available when Azure IaaS was released.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-427">每個單一 VHD 會強制執行 IOPS 配額。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-427">There were IOPS quotas enforced per single VHD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-428">發生延遲不是在相同類別，如 SAN/NAS 裝置通常會部署為高階的 SAP 系統裝載在內部部署的 hello。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-428">Latency experienced was not in hello same class as SAN/NAS devices typically deployed for high-end SAP systems hosted on-premises.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-429">不過，標準儲存體 Azure 證實足以應付數以百計的 hello 同時部署在 Azure 中 SAP 系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-429">Nevertheless, hello Azure Standard Storage proved sufficient for many hundreds SAP systems meanwhile deployed in Azure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-430">Azure 的標準儲存體計費根據 hello 實際儲存的資料，hello 磁碟區的儲存體交易、 傳出資料傳輸與選擇的備援性選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-430">Azure Standard Storage is charged based on hello actual data that is stored, hello volume of storage transactions, outbound data transfers and redundancy option chosen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-431">可以在 hello 大 1 TB 的大小，建立多 Vhd，但只要維持空白會產生任何費用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-431">Many VHDs can be created at hello maximum 1TB in size, but as long as those remain empty there is no charge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-432">接著，您就會填入一個 100 gb VHD，如果您將支付儲存 100 GB，不能用於建立 vhd 與 hello 名義大小 hello。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-432">If you then fill one VHD with 100GB each, you will be charged for storing 100GB and not for hello nominal size hello VHD got created with.</span></span>

#### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-433"><a name="ff5ad0f9-f7f4-4022-9102-af07aef3bc92"></a>Azure 進階儲存體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-433"><a name="ff5ad0f9-f7f4-4022-9102-af07aef3bc92"></a>Azure Premium Storage</span></span>

##### <a name="azure-virtual-networks"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-494">Azure 虛擬網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-494">Azure Virtual Networks</span></span>

#### <a name="private-connection-tooazure--expressroute"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-560">私用連接 tooAzure – ExpressRoute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-560">Private Connection tooAzure – ExpressRoute</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-561">Microsoft Azure ExpressRoute 可讓 hello 建立私人連線 Azure 資料中心與任一 hello 客戶的內部部署基礎結構之間部署或共置環境中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-561">Microsoft Azure ExpressRoute allows hello creation of private connections between Azure data centers and either hello customer's on-premises infrastructure or in a co-location environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-562">ExpressRoute 是由各種 MPLS (封包交換式) VPN 提供者或其他網路服務提供者所提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-562">ExpressRoute is offered by various MPLS (packet switched) VPN providers or other Network Service Providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-563">ExpressRoute 連線不會經過 hello 公用網際網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-563">ExpressRoute connections do not go over hello public Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-564">ExpressRoute 連線 hello 網際網路提供較高的安全性、 透過多個並聯電路、 速度和低延遲比一般的連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-564">ExpressRoute connections offer higher security, more reliability through multiple parallel circuits, faster speeds and lower latencies than typical connections over hello Internet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-565">如需 Azure ExpressRoute 和供應項目的詳細資訊，請參閱︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-565">Find more details on Azure ExpressRoute and offerings here:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-567"><https://azure.microsoft.com/pricing/details/expressroute/></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-567"><https://azure.microsoft.com/pricing/details/expressroute/></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-569">如下方所記載，Express Route 可透過一個 ExpressRoute 循環來啟用多個 Azure 訂用帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-569">Express Route enables multiple Azure subscriptions through one ExpressRoute circuit as documented here</span></span>

#### <a name="forced-tunneling-in-case-of-cross-premises"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-572">跨單位時的強制通道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-572">Forced tunneling in case of cross-premises</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-573">對於 Vm 加入內部部署網域透過站對站、 點對站或 ExpressRoute，您需要 toomake 確定也對這些 Vm 中的所有 hello 使用者會取得都部署 hello 網際網路 proxy 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-573">For VMs joining on-premises domains through site-to-site, point-to-site or ExpressRoute, you need toomake sure that hello Internet proxy settings are getting deployed for all hello users in those VMs as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-574">根據預設，這些 Vm 或使用者使用瀏覽器 tooaccess hello 網際網路不會透過 hello 公司 proxy，但會直接透過 Azure toohello 連接中執行的軟體網際網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-574">By default, software running in those VMs or users using a browser tooaccess hello internet would not go through hello company proxy, but would connect straight through Azure toohello internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-575">但即使 hello proxy 設定不是 100%的解決方案 toodirect hello 流量透過 hello 公司 proxy 因為負責軟體與服務 toocheck hello proxy。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-575">But even hello proxy setting is not a 100% solution toodirect hello traffic through hello company proxy since it is responsibility of software and services toocheck for hello proxy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-576">如果 hello VM 中執行的軟體沒有這樣做，或有系統管理員操作 hello 設定，可以再次繞道流量 toohello 網際網路直接透過 Azure toohello 網際網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-576">If software running in hello VM is not doing that or an administrator manipulates hello settings, traffic toohello Internet can be detoured again directly through Azure toohello Internet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-577">在這排序 tooavoid 中，您可以設定強制通道與內部部署與 Azure 之間的站對站連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-577">In order tooavoid this, you can configure Forced Tunneling with site-to-site connectivity between on-premises and Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-578">hello hello 強制通道功能的詳細的說明發行這裡<https://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/vpn-gateway-forced-tunneling-rm/></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-578">hello detailed description of hello Forced Tunneling feature is published here <https://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/vpn-gateway-forced-tunneling-rm/></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-579">透過 ExpressRoute 強制的通道會啟用客戶透過 ExpressRoute BGP hello 將預設路由通告對等互連工作階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-579">Forced Tunneling with ExpressRoute is enabled by customers advertising a default route via hello ExpressRoute BGP peering sessions.</span></span>

### <a name="quotas-in-azure-virtual-machine-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-587">Azure 虛擬機器服務中的配額</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-587">Quotas in Azure Virtual Machine Services</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-588">我們需要 toobe 清除有關 hello 事實，hello 儲存，並在 hello Azure 基礎結構中執行各種服務的 Vm 之間會共用網路基礎結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-588">We need toobe clear about hello fact that hello storage and network infrastructure is shared between VMs running a variety of services in hello Azure infrastructure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-589">如同 hello 客戶自己的資料中心，過度佈建一些 hello 基礎結構資源採用位置 tooa 程度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-589">And just as in hello customer’s own data centers, over-provisioning of some of hello infrastructure resources does take place tooa degree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-590">hello Microsoft Azure 平台會使用磁碟、 CPU、 網路和其他配額 toolimit hello 資源耗用量和 toopreserve 一致和確定的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-590">hello Microsoft Azure Platform uses disk, CPU, network and other quotas toolimit hello resource consumption and toopreserve consistent and deterministic performance.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-591">hello 不同 VM 類型 （A5、 A6 等） 會有不同的磁碟、 CPU、 RAM 和網路的 hello 數目的配額。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-591">hello different VM types (A5, A6, etc) have different quotas for hello number of disks, CPU, RAM and Network.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-592">SAP 所支援的 hello VM 類型的 CPU 和記憶體資源上會預先配置 hello 主機節點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-592">CPU and memory resources of hello VM types supported by SAP are pre-allocated on hello host nodes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-593">這表示 hello VM 部署之後，hello hello 主機上的資源將會使用 hello VM 類型所定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-593">This means that once hello VM is deployed, hello resources on hello host will be available as defined by hello VM type.</span></span>
>
>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-594">您必須考量時，規劃和調整 SAP Azure 解決方案上 hello 每種虛擬機器大小的配額。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-594">When planning and sizing SAP on Azure solutions hello quotas for each virtual machine size must be considered.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-595">說明 hello VM 配額[這裡][virtual-machines-sizes]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-595">hello VM quotas are described [here][virtual-machines-sizes].</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-596">所述的 hello 配額代表 hello 理論上的最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-596">hello quotas described represent hello theoretical maximum values.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-597">每個 VHD 的 IOPS 的 hello 限制可能達到較小 Io (8kb)，但可能可能無法達到較大 Io (1mb)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-597">hello limit of IOPS per VHD may be achieved with small IOs (8kb) but possibly may not be achieved with large IOs (1Mb).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-598">hello IOPS 限制為單一 vhd 的 hello 資料粒度上強制執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-598">hello IOPS limit is enforced on hello granularity of single VHDs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-599">為初步決策樹狀結構 toodecide 是否 SAP 系統整合到 Azure 虛擬機器服務和其功能或現有的系統必須 toobe 中訂單 toodeploy hello 系統在 Azure 上，以不同的方式設定是否可以使用下列 hello 決策樹：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-599">As a rough decision tree toodecide whether an SAP system fits into Azure Virtual Machine Services and its capabilities or whether an existing system needs toobe configured differently in order toodeploy hello system on Azure, hello decision tree below can be used:</span></span>

If none of hello SAP supported Azure VM types can deliver hello required SAPS, hello workload of hello planned SAP system can’t be run on Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-614">您必須 toodeploy hello 系統在內部部署或 hello 系統所需 toochange hello 工作負載磁碟區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-614">You either need toodeploy hello system on-premises or you need toochange hello workload volume for hello system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-615">**步驟 4**︰如[這裡][virtual-machines-sizes]所述，不論您使用的是「標準儲存體」還是「進階儲存體」，Azure 都會針對每個 VHD 強制執行 IOPS 配額。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-615">**Step 4**: As documented [here][virtual-machines-sizes], Azure enforces an IOPS quota per VHD independent whether you use Standard Storage or Premium Storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-616">視 VM 類型 hello hello 可掛接的 Vhd 數目而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-616">Dependent on hello VM type, hello number of VHDs which can be mounted varies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-617">如此一來，您可以計算與每個 hello 不同 VM 類型可達到 IOPS 數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-617">As a result, you can calculate a maximum IOPS number that can be achieved with each of hello different VM types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-618">相依於 hello 資料庫檔案配置，您可以等量分割 Vhd toobecome 一個磁碟區 hello 客體作業系統中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-618">Dependent on hello database file layout, you can stripe VHDs toobecome one volume in hello guest OS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-619">不過，如果 hello 目前 IOPS 磁碟區已部署的 SAP 系統超過 hello 最大 VM 類型的 Azure，而且如果沒有更多的記憶體使用沒有機會 toocompensate hello 計算限制，hello 的 hello SAP 系統的工作負載可能會影響嚴重。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-619">However, if hello current IOPS volume of a deployed SAP system exceeds hello calculated limits of hello largest VM type of Azure and if there is no chance toocompensate with more memory, hello workload of hello SAP system can be impacted severely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-620">在這種情況下，您可以按其中則不應部署在 Azure 上的 hello 系統的點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-620">In such cases, you can hit a point where you should not deploy hello system on Azure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-621">**步驟 5**： 特別是在 SAP 系統部署在內部 2 層組態中，hello 機會 hello 系統，可能需要 toobe 3 層組態中設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-621">**Step 5**: Especially in SAP systems which are deployed on-premises in 2-Tier configurations, hello chances are that hello system might need toobe configured on Azure in a 3-Tier configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-622">在此步驟中，您會需要 toocheck 中是否有元件 hello SAP 應用程式層的無法擴充，以及這不會放入 hello CPU 和記憶體資源 hello 不同 Azure VM 類型提供項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-622">In this step, you need toocheck whether there is a component in hello SAP application layer which can’t be scaled out and which would not fit into hello CPU and memory resources hello different Azure VM types offer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-623">如果確實有這類元件，hello SAP 系統和其工作負載無法部署到 Azure。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-623">If there indeed is such a component, hello SAP system and its workload can’t be deployed into Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-624">但如果您可以向外延展 hello 到多個 Azure Vm，hello 系統的元件可以部署到 Azure 的 SAP 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-624">But if you can scale-out hello SAP application components into multiple Azure VMs, hello system can be deployed into Azure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-625">**步驟 6**: hello DBMS 和 SAP 應用程式層元件可以在 Azure Vm 中執行，如果需要 toobe 定義與 hello 組態：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-625">**Step 6**: If hello DBMS and SAP application layer components can be run in Azure VMs, hello configuration needs toobe defined with regard to:</span></span>

## <a name="managing-azure-assets"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-629">管理 Azure 資產</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-629">Managing Azure Assets</span></span>
### <a name="azure-portal"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-630">Azure 入口網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-630">Azure Portal</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-631">hello Azure 入口網站是一個三個介面 toomanage Azure VM 部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-631">hello Azure Portal is one of three interfaces toomanage Azure VM deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-632">hello 基本管理工作，例如從映像，來部署 Vm 可以透過 hello Azure 入口網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-632">hello basic management tasks, like deploying VMs from images, can be done through hello Azure Portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-633">此外，hello 建立儲存體帳戶、 虛擬網路和其他 Azure 元件也會是工作 hello Azure 入口網站可妥善處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-633">In addition, hello creation of Storage Accounts, Virtual Networks and other Azure components are also tasks hello Azure Portal can handle very well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-634">不過，像是將 Vhd 從上傳內部 tooAzure 或 Azure 內複製 VHD 所需要協力廠商工具或透過 PowerShell 或 CLI 管理工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-634">However, functionality like uploading VHDs from on-premises tooAzure or copying a VHD within Azure are tasks which require either third party tools or administration through PowerShell or CLI.</span></span>

#### <a name="copying-sap-systems-within-azure"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-868">在 Azure 內複製 SAP 系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-868">Copying SAP systems within Azure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-873">**結論： 順序 toocopy] 或 [儲存 Vhd 的一部分的 SAP 系統設定您需要 toostop hello SAP 系統，而且也需要向 hello tooshut 部署 VM。只有然後您可以複製或下載 Vhd tooeither hello 組建立在 Azure 或內部部署的 hello SAP 系統的複本。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-873">**Conclusion: In order toocopy or save VHDs which are part of an SAP system configuration you need toostop hello SAP system and also need tooshut down hello deployed VM. ##### <a name="powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-889">Powershell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-889">Powershell</span></span>
```powershell
# attach a vhd tooa vm
$vm = Get-AzureRmVM -ResourceGroupName <resource group name> -Name <vm name>
$vm = Add-AzureRmVMDataDisk -VM $vm -Name newdatadisk -VhdUri <path toovhd> -Caching <caching option> -DiskSizeInGB $null -Lun <lun e.g. 0> -CreateOption attach
$vm | Update-AzureRmVM

# attach a copy of hello vhd tooa vm
$vm = Get-AzureRmVM -ResourceGroupName <resource group name> -Name <vm name>
$vm = Add-AzureRmVMDataDisk -VM $vm -Name newdatadisk -VhdUri <new path of vhd> -SourceImageUri <path tooimage vhd> -Caching <caching option> -DiskSizeInGB $null -Lun <lun e.g. 0> -CreateOption fromImage
$vm | Update-AzureRmVM
```

```
# attach a vhd tooa vm
azure vm disk attach <resource group name> <vm name> <path toovhd>
```

#### <a name="disk-handling"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-957">磁碟處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-957">Disk Handling</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-963">**請注意**: Vhd 在任何給定時間只能附加的 tooone VM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-963">**Note**: VHDs can only be attached tooone VM at any given time.</span></span>

##### <a name="powershell"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1069">Powershell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1069">Powershell</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1070">為每個訓練/示範環境建立新的資源群組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1070">Create a new resoure group for every training/demo landscape</span></span>

```powershell
$rgName = "SAPERPDemo1"
New-AzureRmResourceGroup -Name $rgName -Location "North Europe"
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1071">建立新的儲存體帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1071">Create a new storage account</span></span>

```powershell
$suffix = Get-Random -Minimum 100000 -Maximum 999999

```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1072">建立新的虛擬網路 hello 每個訓練/示範橫向 tooenable hello 使用相同的主機名稱和 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1072">Create a new virtual network for every training/demo landscape tooenable hello usage of hello same hostname and IP addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1073">網路安全性群組，只允許流量 tooport 3389 tooenable 遠端桌面存取和連接埠 22 SSH 受 hello 虛擬網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1073">hello virtual network is protected by a Network Security Group that only allows traffic tooport 3389 tooenable Remote Desktop access and port 22 for SSH.</span></span>

```powershell
# Create a new Virtual Network
$rdpRule = New-AzureRmNetworkSecurityRuleConfig -Name SAPERPDemoNSGRDP -Protocol * -SourcePortRange * -DestinationPortRange 3389 -Access Allow -Direction Inbound -SourceAddressPrefix * -DestinationAddressPrefix * -Priority 100
$sshRule = New-AzureRmNetworkSecurityRuleConfig -Name SAPERPDemoNSGSSH -Protocol * -SourcePortRange * -DestinationPortRange 22 -Access Allow -Direction Inbound -SourceAddressPrefix * -DestinationAddressPrefix * -Priority 101
$nsg = New-AzureRmNetworkSecurityGroup -Name SAPERPDemoNSG -ResourceGroupName $rgName -Location  "North Europe" -SecurityRules $rdpRule,$sshRule

$subnetConfig = New-AzureRmVirtualNetworkSubnetConfig -Name Subnet1 -AddressPrefix  10.0.1.0/24 -NetworkSecurityGroup $nsg
$vnet = New-AzureRmVirtualNetwork -Name SAPERPDemoVNet -ResourceGroupName $rgName -Location "North Europe"  -AddressPrefix 10.0.1.0/24 -Subnet $subnetConfig
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1074">建立新的公用 IP 位址可能是使用的 tooaccess hello 虛擬機器從 hello 網際網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1074">Create a new public IP address that can be used tooaccess hello virtual machine from hello internet</span></span>

```powershell
# Create a public IP address with a DNS name
$pip = New-AzureRmPublicIpAddress -Name SAPERPDemoPIP -ResourceGroupName $rgName -Location "North Europe" -DomainNameLabel $rgName.ToLower() -AllocationMethod Dynamic
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1075">建立新的網路介面 hello 虛擬機器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1075">Create a new network interface for hello virtual machine</span></span>

```powershell
# Create a new Network Interface
$nic = New-AzureRmNetworkInterface -Name SAPERPDemoNIC -ResourceGroupName $rgName -Location "North Europe" -Subnet $vnet.Subnets[0] -PublicIpAddress $pip
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1076">建立虛擬機器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1076">Create a virtual machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1077">Hello 僅限雲端案例中每個 VM 都有 hello 相同的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1077">For hello Cloud-Only scenario every VM will have hello same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1078">hello hello 這些 Vm 中的執行個體將會是 SAP NetWeaver 的 SAP SID hello 相同也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1078">hello SAP SID of hello SAP NetWeaver instances in those VMs will be hello same as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1079">內 hello Azure 資源群組，hello hello VM 名稱需要 toobe 唯一的但您可以在不同的 Azure 資源群組中執行 Vm 以 hello 相同的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1079">Within hello Azure Resource Group, hello name of hello VM needs toobe unique, but in different Azure Resource Groups you can run VMs with hello same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1080">hello 預設 'Administrator' 帳戶的 Windows 或 linux 的 ' root' 不是有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1080">hello default 'Administrator' account of Windows or 'root' for Linux are not valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1081">因此，新的系統管理員使用者名稱需要 toobe 定義連同密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1081">Therefore, a new administrator user name needs toobe defined together with a password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1082">hello hello VM 大小也需要定義 toobe。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1082">hello size of hello VM also needs toobe defined.</span></span>

```powershell
#####
# Create a new virtual machine with an official image from hello Azure Marketplace
#####
$cred=Get-Credential -Message "Type hello name and password of hello local administrator account."
$vmconfig = New-AzureRmVMConfig -VMName SAPERPDemo -VMSize Standard_D11

# select image
$vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMSourceImage -VM $vmconfig -PublisherName "MicrosoftWindowsServer" -Offer "WindowsServer" -Skus "2012-R2-Datacenter" -Version "latest"
$vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMOperatingSystem -VM $vmconfig -Windows -ComputerName "SAPERPDemo" -Credential $cred -ProvisionVMAgent -EnableAutoUpdate
# $vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMSourceImage -VM $vmconfig -PublisherName "SUSE" -Offer "SLES" -Skus "12" -Version "latest"
# $vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMSourceImage -VM $vmconfig -PublisherName "RedHat" -Offer "RHEL" -Skus "7.2" -Version "latest"
# $vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMOperatingSystem -VM $vmconfig -Linux -ComputerName "SAPERPDemo" -Credential $cred

$vmconfig = Add-AzureRmVMNetworkInterface -VM $vmconfig -Id $nic.Id

$diskName="os"
$osDiskUri=$account.PrimaryEndpoints.Blob.ToString() + "vhds/" + $diskName  + ".vhd"
$vmconfig = Set-AzureRmVMOSDisk -VM $vmconfig -Name $diskName -VhdUri $osDiskUri -CreateOption fromImage
$vm = New-AzureRmVM -ResourceGroupName $rgName -Location "North Europe" -VM $vmconfig
```

```powershell
#####
# Create a new virtual machine with a VHD that contains hello private image that you want toouse
#####
$cred=Get-Credential -Message "Type hello name and password of hello local administrator account."
$vmconfig = New-AzureRmVMConfig -VMName SAPERPDemo -VMSize Standard_D11

$vmconfig = Add-AzureRmVMNetworkInterface -VM $vmconfig -Id $nic.Id

$diskName="osfromimage"
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1083">選擇性地新增其他磁碟，並還原所需的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1083">Optionally add additional disks and restore necessary content.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1084">請注意，所有 blob 名稱 (Url toohello blob) 必須都是在 Azure 中獨一無二。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1084">Be aware that all blob names (URLs toohello blobs) must be unique within Azure.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1089">建立新的儲存體帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1089">Create a new storage account</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1090">建立新的虛擬網路 hello 每個訓練/示範橫向 tooenable hello 使用相同的主機名稱和 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1090">Create a new virtual network for every training/demo landscape tooenable hello usage of hello same hostname and IP addresses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1091">網路安全性群組，只允許流量 tooport 3389 tooenable 遠端桌面存取和連接埠 22 SSH 受 hello 虛擬網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1091">hello virtual network is protected by a Network Security Group that only allows traffic tooport 3389 tooenable Remote Desktop access and port 22 for SSH.</span></span>

```
azure network nsg create --resource-group $rgName --location "North Europe" --name SAPERPDemoNSG
azure network nsg rule create --resource-group $rgName --nsg-name SAPERPDemoNSG --name SAPERPDemoNSGRDP --protocol \* --source-address-prefix \* --source-port-range \* --destination-address-prefix \* --destination-port-range 3389 --access Allow --priority 100 --direction Inbound

azure network vnet create --resource-group $rgName --name SAPERPDemoVNet --location "North Europe" --address-prefixes 10.0.1.0/24
```

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1092">建立新的公用 IP 位址可能是使用的 tooaccess hello 虛擬機器從 hello 網際網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1092">Create a new public IP address that can be used tooaccess hello virtual machine from hello internet</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1093">建立新的網路介面 hello 虛擬機器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1093">Create a new network interface for hello virtual machine</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1094">建立虛擬機器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1094">Create a virtual machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1095">Hello 僅限雲端案例中每個 VM 都有 hello 相同的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1095">For hello Cloud-Only scenario every VM will have hello same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1096">hello hello 這些 Vm 中的執行個體將會是 SAP NetWeaver 的 SAP SID hello 相同也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1096">hello SAP SID of hello SAP NetWeaver instances in those VMs will be hello same as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1097">內 hello Azure 資源群組，hello hello VM 名稱需要 toobe 唯一的但您可以在不同的 Azure 資源群組中執行 Vm 以 hello 相同的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1097">Within hello Azure Resource Group, hello name of hello VM needs toobe unique, but in different Azure Resource Groups you can run VMs with hello same name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1098">hello 預設 'Administrator' 帳戶的 Windows 或 linux 的 ' root' 不是有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1098">hello default 'Administrator' account of Windows or 'root' for Linux are not valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1099">因此，新的系統管理員使用者名稱需要 toobe 定義連同密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1099">Therefore, a new administrator user name needs toobe defined together with a password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1100">hello hello VM 大小也需要定義 toobe。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1100">hello size of hello VM also needs toobe defined.</span></span>

## <a name="supportability"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1295">支援能力</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1295">Supportability</span></span>
### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1296"><a name="6f0a47f3-a289-4090-a053-2521618a28c3"></a>適用於 SAP 的 Azure 監視解決方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1296"><a name="6f0a47f3-a289-4090-a053-2521618a28c3"></a>Azure Monitoring Solution for SAP</span></span>

#### <a name="solution-design"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1300">解決方案設計</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1300">Solution design</span></span>
