## <a name="high-availability-ha-and-disaster-recovery-dr-for-sap-netweaver-running-on-azure-virtual-machines"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1350">Azure 虛擬機器上執行之 SAP NetWeaver 的高可用性 (HA) 和災害復原 (DR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1350">High Availability (HA) and Disaster Recovery (DR) for SAP NetWeaver running on Azure Virtual Machines</span></span>
### <a name="definition-of-terminologies"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1351">術語定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1351">Definition of terminologies</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1352">hello 詞彙**高可用性 (HA)**通常相關的 tooa 設定的技術，藉由提供業務續航力透過 IT 服務，IT 中斷情況降到最低備援、 容錯或容錯移轉受保護的元件在 hello**相同**資料中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1352">hello Term **high availability (HA)** is generally related tooa set of technologies that minimizes IT disruptions by providing business continuity of IT services through redundant, fault-tolerant or failover protected components inside hello **same** data center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1353">在本例中，會是在一個 Azure 區域內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1353">In our case, within one Azure Region.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1354">**災害復原 (DR)** 的目標也是將 IT 服務中斷的情況降到最低，但其復原通常會橫跨距離數百公里遠的**不同**資料中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1354">**Disaster recovery (DR)** is also targeting minimizing IT services disruption, and their recovery but across **different** data centers, that are usually located hundreds of kilometers away.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1355">在我們的案例通常 hello 不同 Azure 區域間相同地理政治地區或客戶為您所建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1355">In our case usually between different Azure Regions within hello same geopolitical region or as established by you as a customer.</span></span>

### <a name="overview-of-high-availability"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1356">高可用性概觀</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1356">Overview of High Availability</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1357">我們可以分隔 hello 討論 SAP 中的高可用性 Azure 分成兩個部分：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1357">We can separate hello discussion about SAP high availability in Azure into two parts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1358">**Azure 基礎結構高可用性**(例如計算 (VM)、網路、儲存體等的 HA)，以及它在增加 SAP 應用程式可用性方面的優點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1358">**Azure infrastructure high availability**, e.g. HA of compute (VMs), network, storage etc. and its benefits for increasing SAP application availability.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1359">**SAP 應用程式高可用性**(例如 SAP 軟體元件的 HA)︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1359">**SAP application high availability**, e.g. HA of SAP software components:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1360">SAP 應用程式伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1360">SAP application servers</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1361">SAP ASCS/SCS 執行個體</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1361">SAP ASCS/SCS instance</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1362">DB 伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1362">DB server</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1363">以及如何與 Azure 基礎結構 HA 結合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1363">and how it can be combined with Azure infrastructure HA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1364">在 Azure 中 SAP 高可用性有一些差異比較 tooSAP 高可用性的內部部署實體或虛擬環境中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1364">SAP High Availability in Azure has some differences compared tooSAP High Availability in an on-premises physical or virtual environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1365">hello 從 SAP 的下列文件描述在 Windows 上的虛擬化環境中的標準 SAP 高可用性組態： <http://scn.sap.com/docs/DOC-44415>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1365">hello following paper from SAP describes standard SAP High Availability configurations in virtualized environments on Windows: <http://scn.sap.com/docs/DOC-44415>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1366">不同於 Windows，Linux 沒有整合 sapinst 的 SAP-HA 組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1366">There is no sapinst-integrated SAP-HA configuration for Linux like it exists for Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1367">如需有關 Linux 之內部部署 SAP HA 的詳細資訊，請參閱︰<http://scn.sap.com/docs/DOC-8541>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1367">Regarding SAP HA on-premises for Linux find more information here : <http://scn.sap.com/docs/DOC-8541>.</span></span>

### <a name="azure-infrastructure-high-availability"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1368">Azure 基礎結構高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1368">Azure Infrastructure High Availability</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1369">Azure 虛擬機器上目前沒有任何單一 VM SLA 可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1369">There is no single-VM SLA available on Azure Virtual Machines right now.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1370">tooget 了解如何在單一 VM 的 hello 可用性看起來就像是只可以建立 hello 產品的 hello 不同可用的 Azure Sla: <https://azure.microsoft.com/support/legal/sla/>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1370">tooget an idea how hello availability of a single VM might look like you can simply build hello product of hello different available Azure SLAs: <https://azure.microsoft.com/support/legal/sla/>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1371">hello 計算 hello 基礎都是 30 天內每月或 43200 分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1371">hello basis for hello calculation is 30 days per month, or 43200 minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1372">因此，0.05%停機對應 too21.6 分鐘的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1372">Therefore, 0.05% downtime corresponds too21.6 minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1373">像往常一樣，hello hello 不同服務可用性會乘以 hello 遵循方法中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1373">As usual, hello availability of hello different services will multiply in hello following way:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1374">(可用性服務 #1/100) * (可用性服務 #2/100) * (可用性服務 #3/100) *...</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1374">(Availability Service #1/100) * (Availability Service #2/100) * (Availability Service #3/100) *…</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1375">例如：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1375">Like:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1376">(99.95/100) * (99.9/100) * (99.9/100) = 0.9975 或整體可用性 99.75%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1376">(99.95/100) * (99.9/100) * (99.9/100) = 0.9975 or an overall availability of 99.75%.</span></span>

#### <a name="virtual-machine-vm-high-availability"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1377">虛擬機器 (VM) 高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1377">Virtual Machine (VM) High Availability</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1378">Azure 平台事件可能會影響 hello 可用性的虛擬機器的兩種類型： 維護與非計劃性的維護計畫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1378">There are two types of Azure platform events that can affect hello availability of your virtual machines: planned maintenance and unplanned maintenance.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1379">規劃的維護事件會定期更新由 Microsoft toohello 基礎 Azure 平台 tooimprove 整體的可靠性、 效能和安全性的虛擬機器執行的 hello 平台基礎結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1379">Planned maintenance events are periodic updates made by Microsoft toohello underlying Azure platform tooimprove overall reliability, performance, and security of hello platform infrastructure that your virtual machines run on.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1380">當 hello 硬體或基礎虛擬機器的實體基礎結構發生某種錯誤時，就會發生非計劃性的維護事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1380">Unplanned maintenance events occur when hello hardware or physical infrastructure underlying your virtual machine has faulted in some way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1381">這可能包含本機網路錯誤、本機磁碟錯誤，或其他機架層級的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1381">This may include local network failures, local disk failures, or other rack level failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1382">偵測到這類失敗時，hello Azure 平台會自動移轉虛擬機器從 hello 狀況不良的實體伺服器主控虛擬機器 tooa 狀況良好實體伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1382">When such a failure is detected, hello Azure platform will automatically migrate your virtual machine from hello unhealthy physical server hosting your virtual machine tooa healthy physical server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1383">這類事件很少見，但也可能會造成虛擬機器 tooreboot。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1383">Such events are rare, but may also cause your virtual machine tooreboot.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1384">如需更多詳細資訊，請參閱這份文件︰<http://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/virtual-machines-manage-availability></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1384">More details can be found in this documentation: <http://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/virtual-machines-manage-availability></span></span>

#### <a name="azure-storage-redundancy"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1385">Azure 儲存體備援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1385">Azure Storage Redundancy</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1386">Microsoft Azure 儲存體帳戶中的 hello 資料會一直複寫的 tooensure 耐久性與高可用性，會議 hello Azure 儲存體 SLA，即使在 hello 字體的暫時性硬體失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1386">hello data in your Microsoft Azure Storage Account is always replicated tooensure durability and high availability, meeting hello Azure Storage SLA even in hello face of transient hardware failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1387">由於 Azure 儲存體而導致 3 映像的 hello 資料依預設，就不需要 RAID5 或 RAID1 跨多個 Azure 磁碟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1387">Since Azure Storage is keeping 3 images of hello data by default, RAID5 or RAID1 across multiple Azure disks are not necessary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1388">如需更多詳細資訊，請參閱這篇文章︰<http://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/storage-redundancy/></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1388">More details can be found in this article: <http://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/storage-redundancy/></span></span>

#### <a name="utilizing-azure-infrastructure-vm-restart-tooachieve-higher-availability-of-sap-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1389">利用 Azure 基礎結構 VM 重新啟動 tooAchieve 的 SAP 應用程式的 「 高可用性 」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1389">Utilizing Azure Infrastructure VM Restart tooAchieve “Higher Availability” of SAP Applications</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1390">如果您決定不 toouse 功能類似 Windows Server 容錯移轉叢集 (WSFC) 或 Linux 的對等 (hello 後者一個尚不支援在 Azure SAP 軟體的結合)、 Azure VM 重新啟動是利用的 tooprotect SAP 系統，以防計劃和hello Azure 的實體伺服器基礎結構及整體基礎的 Azure 平台的非計劃性的停機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1390">If you decide not toouse functionalities like Windows Server Failover Clustering (WSFC) or a Linux equivalent ( hello latter one is not supported yet on Azure in combination with SAP software ), Azure VM Restart is utilized tooprotect a SAP System against planned and unplanned downtime of hello Azure physical server infrastructure and overall underlying Azure platform.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1391">重要 toomention Vm 並不是應用程式，將 Azure VM 重新啟動主要保護它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1391">It is important toomention that Azure VM Restart primarily protects VMs and NOT applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1392">VM 重新啟動並未提供 SAP 應用程式的高可用性，而是提供特定基礎結構層級的可用性，因而間接達到 SAP 系統的「更高可用性」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1392">VM Restart does not offer high availability for SAP applications, but it does offer a certain level of infrastructure availability and therefore indirectly “higher availability” of SAP systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1393">另外還有任何 SLA 的 hello 花費的時間 toorestart VM 主機計劃性或非計劃性中斷後。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1393">There is also no SLA for hello time it will take toorestart a VM after a planned or unplanned host outage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1394">因此，此「高可用性」方法不適用於 SAP 系統的重要元件，例如 (A)SCS 或 DBMS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1394">Therefore, this method of ‘high availability’ is not suitable for critical components of a SAP system like (A)SCS or DBMS.</span></span>
>
>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1395">高可用性的另一個重要基礎結構項目是儲存體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1395">Another important infrastructure element for high availability is storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1396">例如</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1396">E.g.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1397">Azure 儲存體 SLA 可用性為 99,9%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1397">Azure Storage SLA is 99,9 % availability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1398">如果使用者將所有 VM 及其磁碟部署到單一 Azure 儲存體帳戶，當 Azure 儲存體可能無法使用時，將會導致 Azure 儲存體帳戶中的所有 VM，以及這些 VM 內執行的所有 SAP 元件都無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1398">If one deploys all VMs with its disks into a single Azure Storage Account, potential Azure Storage unavailability will cause unavailability of all VMs that are placed in that Azure Storage Account, and also all SAP components running inside of those VMs.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1399">您也可以針對每個 VM 使用專用儲存體帳戶，而不是將所有 VM 放入單一 Azure 儲存體帳戶；如此一來，您就可以藉由使用多個獨立的 Azure 儲存體帳戶，來增加整體 VM 和 SAP 應用程式可用性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1399">Instead of putting all VMs into one single Azure Storage Account, you can also use dedicated storage accounts for each VM, and in this way increase overall VM and SAP application availability by using multiple independent Azure Storage Accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1400">使用 Azure 基礎結構 HA 之 SAP NetWeaver 系統的範例架構如下所示︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1400">A sample architecture of a SAP NetWeaver system that uses Azure infrastructure HA could look like this:</span></span>

![利用 Azure 基礎結構 HA tooachieve SAP 應用程式 「 較高 」 的可用性][planning-guide-figure-2900]

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1402">重要的 SAP 元件我們所達成 hello 遵循為止：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1402">For critical SAP components we achieved hello following so far :</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1403">SAP 應用程式伺服器 (AS) 的高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1403">High Availability of SAP Application Servers (AS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1404">SAP 應用程式伺服器執行個體是備援元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1404">SAP application server instances are redundant components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1405">每個 SAP AS 執行個體都是部署在自己的 VM 上，而此 VM 是在不同的 Azure「容錯網域」及「升級網域」中執行 (請參閱[容錯網域][planning-guide-3.2.1]和[升級網域][planning-guide-3.2.2]章節)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1405">Each SAP AS instance is deployed on its own VM, that is running in a different Azure Fault and Upgrade Domain (see chapters [Fault Domains][planning-guide-3.2.1] and [Upgrade Domains][planning-guide-3.2.2]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1406">這是藉由使用「Azure 可用性設定組」來加以確保 (請參閱 [Azure 可用性設定組][planning-guide-3.2.3]一章)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1406">This is ensured by using Azure Availability Sets (see chapter [Azure Availability Sets][planning-guide-3.2.3]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1407">當 Azure 容錯或升級網域可能因規劃或未規劃而無法使用時，將會導致有限數目的 VM 及其 SAP AS 執行個體無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1407">Potential planned or unplanned unavailability of an Azure Fault or Upgrade Domain will cause unavailability of a restricted number of VMs with their SAP AS instances.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1408">每個 SAP 執行個體都會在自己的 Azure 儲存體帳戶中 - 當一個 Azure 儲存體可能無法使用時，只會導致一個 VM 及其 SAP AS 執行個體無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1408">Each SAP AS instance is placed in its own Azure Storage account – potential unavailability of one Azure Storage Account will cause unavailability of only one VM with its SAP AS instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1409">不過請注意，一個 Azure 訂用帳戶中的「Azure 儲存體帳戶」數目有限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1409">However, be aware that there is a limit of Azure Storage Accounts within one Azure subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1410">tooensure 自動啟動 (A) SCS 執行個體之後 hello VM 重新開機，請確定 tooset Autostart 參數 (A) SCS 執行個體中的啟動章節所述的設定檔[使用自動啟動 SAP 執行個體][planning-guide-11.5]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1410">tooensure automatic start of (A)SCS instance after hello VM reboot, make sure tooset Autostart parameter in (A)SCS instance start profile described in chapter [Using Autostart for SAP instances][planning-guide-11.5].</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1411">如需更多詳細資料，另請參閱 [SAP 應用程式伺服器的高可用性][planning-guide-11.4.1]一章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1411">Please also read chapter [High Availability for SAP Application Servers][planning-guide-11.4.1] for more details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1412"> SAP (A)SCS 執行個體可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1412">*Higher* Availability of SAP (A)SCS instance</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1413">這裡我們利用 Azure VM 重新啟動 VM 的 tooprotect hello 與已安裝的 SAP (A) SCS 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1413">Here we utilize Azure VM Restart tooprotect hello VM with installed SAP (A)SCS instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1414">在 hello 案例的規劃或未規劃的停機時間的 Azure 伺服器，將重新啟動 Vm，另一個可用的伺服器上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1414">In hello case of planned or unplanned downtime of Azure severs, VMs will be restarted on another available server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1415">如先前所述，Azure VM 重新啟動主要保護 Vm 並不是應用程式時，在此情況下 hello (A) SCS 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1415">As mentioned earlier, Azure VM Restart primarily protects VMs and NOT applications, in this case hello (A)SCS instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1416">透過重新啟動 VM 的 hello 我們將達到間接 SAP (A) SCS 執行個體的 「 高可用性 」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1416">Through hello VM Restart we’ll reach indirectly “higher availability” of SAP (A)SCS instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1417">tooinsure 自動啟動 (A) SCS 執行個體之後 hello VM 重新開機，請確定 tooset Autostart 參數 (A) SCS 執行個體中的啟動章節所述的設定檔[使用自動啟動 SAP 執行個體][planning-guide-11.5]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1417">tooinsure automatic start of (A)SCS instance after hello VM reboot, make sure tooset Autostart parameter in (A)SCS instance start profile described in chapter [Using Autostart for SAP instances][planning-guide-11.5].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1418">這表示 hello (A) SCS 執行個體當做單一失敗點 (SPOF) 執行單一 VM 中的 hello 整個 SAP 環境的 hello 可用性 hello 就因素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1418">This means hello (A)SCS instance as a Single Point of Failure (SPOF) running in a single VM will be hello determinative factor for hello availability of hello whole SAP landscape.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1419"> DBMS 伺服器可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1419">*Higher* Availability of DBMS Server</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1420">在這裡，類似 toohello SAP (A) SCS 執行個體使用的大小寫、 我們利用 Azure VM 重新啟動 tooprotect hello VM 與已安裝的 DBMS 軟體和我們在達到 「 高可用性 」 的 DBMS 軟體透過 VM 重新啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1420">Here, similar toohello SAP (A)SCS instance use case, we utilize Azure VM Restart tooprotect hello VM with installed DBMS software, and we achieve “higher availability” of DBMS software through VM Restart.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1421">單一 VM 中執行 DBMS 也 SPOF，而且它是整個 SAP 環境 hello hello 可用性 hello 就因素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1421">DBMS running in a single VM is also a SPOF, and it is hello determinative factor for hello availability of hello whole SAP landscape.</span></span>

### <a name="sap-application-high-availability-on-azure-iaas"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1422">Azure IaaS 上的 SAP 應用程式高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1422">SAP Application High Availability on Azure IaaS</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1423">tooachieve 完整 SAP 系統高可用性，我們需要 tooprotect 所有關鍵 SAP 系統的元件，例如備援的 SAP 應用程式伺服器，而等唯一元件 （例如單一失敗點） SAP (A) SCS 執行個體和 DBMS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1423">tooachieve full SAP system high availability, we need tooprotect all critical SAP system components, e.g. redundant SAP application servers, and unique components (e.g. Single Point of Failure) like SAP (A)SCS instance and DBMS.</span></span>

#### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1424"><a name="5d9d36f9-9058-435d-8367-5ad05f00de77"></a>SAP 應用程式伺服器的高可用性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1424"><a name="5d9d36f9-9058-435d-8367-5ad05f00de77"></a>High Availability for SAP Application Servers</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1425">Hello SAP 應用程式伺服器/對話執行個體的不必要 toothink 需特定的高可用性解決方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1425">For hello SAP application servers/dialog instances it’s not necessary toothink about a specific high availability solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1426">高可用性可直接透過備援來達成，因此必須在不同的虛擬機器中有足夠的備援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1426">High availability is simply achieved by redundancy and thereby having enough of them in different virtual machines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1427">它們應該全部放在相同 Azure 可用性設定組的 hello Vm tooavoid 可能同時更新 hello hello 計劃性的維護停機期間有相同的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1427">They should all be placed in hello same Azure Availability Set tooavoid that hello VMs might be updated at hello same time during planned maintenance downtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1428">hello 基本功能所建置不同的升級和故障 」 網域在 Azure 的擴充單元已經首見於章[升級 」 網域][planning-guide-3.2.2]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1428">hello basic functionality which builds on different Upgrade and Fault Domains within an Azure Scale Unit was already introduced in chapter [Upgrade Domains][planning-guide-3.2.2].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1429">本文件的 [Azure 可用性設定組][planning-guide-3.2.3]一章則提供「Azure 可用性設定組」的說明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1429">Azure Availability Sets were presented in chapter [Azure Availability Sets][planning-guide-3.2.3] of this document.</span></span>

#### <a name="end-to-end-high-availability-for-hello-complete-sap-system"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1456">端對端的高可用性 hello 完整的 SAP 系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1456">End-to-End High Availability for hello Complete SAP System</span></span>

##### <a name="windowslogowindows-ha-on-windows"></a>![Windows][Logo_Windows] <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1464">Windows 上的 HA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1464">HA on Windows</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1466">下列 Azure 結構 hello 適用於 hello SAP NetWeaver 系統基礎結構問題和主機修補所 toominimize 影響：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1466">hello following Azure constructs are used for hello SAP NetWeaver system, toominimize impact by infrastructure issues and host patching:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1469">hello 完整的系統在一個 Azure 虛擬網路 （必要） 內執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1469">hello complete system runs within one Azure Virtual Network (required).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1470">即使是使用所有的 hello Vm 屬於 toohello hello 的 hello 一個 SAP 系統的 Vm 中的分隔成三個可用性設定組有可能相同的虛擬網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1470">hello separation of hello VMs of one SAP system into three Availability Sets is possible even with all hello VMs belonging toohello same Virtual Network.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1471">執行一個 SAP 系統之 DBMS 執行個體的所有 VM 都會在一個可用性設定組中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1471">All VMs running DBMS instances of one SAP system are in one Availability Set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1472">假設有多個 VM 針對每個系統執行 DBMS 執行個體，因為使用了原生 DBMS 高可用性功能，例如 SQL Server AlwaysOn 或 Oracle Data Guard。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1472">We assume that there is more than one VM running DBMS instances per system since native DBMS high availability features are used, like SQL Server AlwaysOn or Oracle Data Guard.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1473">所有執行 DBMS 執行個體的 VM 都會使用自己的儲存體帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1473">All VMs running DBMS instances use their own storage account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1474">DBMS 資料和記錄檔會從一個儲存體帳戶 tooanother 儲存體帳戶使用 DBMS 高可用性功能 hello 資料同步處理複寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1474">DBMS data and log files are replicated from one storage account tooanother storage account using DBMS high availability functions that synchronize hello data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1475">無法使用的一個儲存體帳戶會導致無法使用的一個 SQL Windows 叢集節點，但不是 hello 整個 SQL Server 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1475">Unavailability of one storage account will cause unavailability of one SQL Windows cluster node, but not hello whole SQL Server service.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1476">執行一個 SAP 系統之 (A)SCS 執行個體的所有 VM 都會在一個可用性設定組中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1476">All VMs running (A)SCS instance of one SAP system are in one Availability Set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1477">這些 Vm 的內部是設定 Windows Server 容錯移轉叢集 (WSFC) tooprotect (A) SCS 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1477">Inside of those VMs is configure Windows Sever Failover Cluster (WSFC) tooprotect (A)SCS instance.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1482">所有的 hello Vm 執行 SAP 應用程式伺服器使用他們自己的儲存體帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1482">ALL hello VMs running SAP application servers use their own storage account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1483">無法使用的一個儲存體帳戶將會造成一個 SAP 應用程式伺服器，讓其他 SAP AS 繼續 toorun 無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1483">Unavailability of one storage account will cause unavailability of one SAP application server, where other SAP AS continue toorun.</span></span>

##### <a name="linuxlogolinux-ha-on-linux"></a>![Linux][Logo_Linux] <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1485">Linux 上的 HA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1485">HA on Linux</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1486">SAP HA 在 Linux on Azure 的 hello 架構基本上是的 hello 與 Windows，做為相同上面所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1486">hello architecture for SAP HA on Linux on Azure is basically hello same as for Windows as described above.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1487">不過截至 2016 年 1 月為止，有兩個限制︰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1487">As of Jan 2016 there are two restrictions though :</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1488">Azure 上的 Linux 目前只支援 SAP ASE 16，而不提供任何 ASE 複寫功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1488">only SAP ASE 16 is currently supported on Linux on Azure without any ASE replication features.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1489">Azure 上的 Linux 尚未支援 SAP (A)SCS HA 解決方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1489">there is no SAP (A)SCS HA solution supported yet on Linux on Azure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1490">因此 SAP Linux Azure 系統無法達成的 2016 年 1 月 hello 做為 SAP Azure 系統的同一個可用性，因為遺漏 HA hello (A) SCS 執行個體和 hello 單一執行個體 SAP ASE 資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1490">As a consequence as of January 2016 a SAP-Linux-Azure system cannot achieve hello same availability as a SAP-Windows-Azure system because of missing HA for hello (A)SCS instance and hello single-instance SAP ASE database.</span></span>

### <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1491"><a name="4e165b58-74ca-474f-a7f4-5e695a93204f"></a>對 SAP 執行個體使用自動啟動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1491"><a name="4e165b58-74ca-474f-a7f4-5e695a93204f"></a>Using Autostart for SAP instances</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1492">SAP 提供 hello OS hello VM 中的 hello 開頭之後立即 hello 功能 toostart SAP 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1492">SAP offered hello functionality toostart SAP instances immediately after hello start of hello OS within hello VM.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1493">hello 確切步驟已記載於 SAP 知識庫文章[1909114] -如何使用 Autostart 參數來自動 toostart SAP 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1493">hello exact steps were documented in  SAP Knowledge Base Article [1909114] - How toostart SAP instances automatically using parameter Autostart.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1494">不過，SAP 不建議您使用 toouse hello 設定，再因為 hello 順序的執行個體重新啟動時，沒有控制項假設影響多個 VM 收到或每個 VM 執行的多個執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1494">However, SAP is not recommending toouse hello setting anymore because there is no control in hello order of instance restarts, assuming more than one VM got affected or multiple instances ran per VM.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1495">假設 Azure 典型案例一個 SAP 應用程式伺服器執行個體的單一 VM，最後會開始重新啟動 VM，hello 案例中，hello Autostart 不是真的很重要，而且可以藉由加入這個參數啟用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1495">Assuming a typical Azure scenario of one SAP application server instance in a VM and hello case of a single VM eventually getting restarted, hello Autostart is not really critical and can be enabled by adding this parameter:</span></span>

    Autostart = 1

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1496">Hello 到啟動 hello SAP ABAP 和/或 Java 執行個體的設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1496">Into hello start profile of hello SAP ABAP and/or Java instance.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1497">hello Autostart 參數可以有以及一些困難。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1497">hello Autostart parameter can have some downfalls as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1498">詳細資料，hello 參數觸發程序 hello 相關 hello 執行個體的 Windows/Linux 服務啟動時 hello 開頭的 SAP ABAP 或 Java 執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1498">In more detail, hello parameter triggers hello start of a SAP ABAP or Java instance when hello related Windows/Linux service of hello instance is started.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1499">這當然是 hello 案例時 hello 作業系統開機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1499">That certainly is hello case when hello operating systems boots up.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1500">不過，SAP 軟體生命週期管理功能 (例如加總或其他更新或升級) 也經常需要重新啟動 SAP 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1500">However, restarts of SAP services are also a common thing for SAP Software Lifecycle Management functionality like SUM or other updates or upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1501">這些功能不預期會自動重新啟動所有執行個體 toobe。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1501">These functionalities are not expecting an instance toobe restarted automatically at all.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1502">因此，hello Autostart 參數應該停用然後再執行這類工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1502">Therefore, hello Autostart parameter should be disabled before running such tasks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1503">hello Autostart 參數也不應該對叢集化，例如 ASCS/SCS/CI SAP 執行個體使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1503">hello Autostart parameter also should not be used for SAP instances that are clustered, like ASCS/SCS/CI.</span></span>

### <a name="larger-3-tier-sap-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1508">更大型的 3 層 SAP 系統</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1508">Larger 3-Tier SAP systems</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1509">稍早的章節中已談到 3 層 SAP 組態的高可用性觀點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1509">High-Availability aspects of 3-Tier SAP configurations got discussed in earlier sections already.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1510">但是，要如何系統 hello DBMS 伺服器要求太大而 toohave 該檔案位於 Azure 中，但無法部署到 Azure 的 hello SAP 應用程式層嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1510">But what about systems where hello DBMS server requirements are too large toohave it located in Azure, but hello SAP application layer could be deployed into Azure?</span></span>

#### <a name="location-of-3-tier-sap-configurations"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1511">3 層 SAP 組態的位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1511">Location of 3-Tier SAP configurations</span></span>

### <a name="offline-backup-of-sap-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1526">SAP 系統的離線備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1526">Offline Backup of SAP systems</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1527">相依於 hello SAP 組態選擇 （2 層或 3 層） 有可能是需要 toobackup。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1527">Dependent on hello SAP configuration chosen (2-Tier or 3-Tier) there could be a need toobackup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1528">hello 內容 hello VM 本身加上 toohave hello 資料庫的備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1528">hello content of hello VM itself plus toohave a backup of hello database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1529">hello DBMS 相關的備份是以資料庫方法預期的 toobe。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1529">hello DBMS related backups are expected toobe done with database methods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1530">Hello 不同資料庫的詳細的說明位於[DBMS 指南][dbms-guide]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1530">A detailed description for hello different databases, can be found in [DBMS Guide][dbms-guide].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1531">在 hello 另一方面，hello SAP 資料可以備份採用離線方式 （包括 hello 資料庫內容） 這一節中所述或線上 hello 下一節中所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1531">On hello other hand, hello SAP data can be backed up in an offline manner (including hello database content as well) as described in this section or online as described in hello next section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1532">hello 離線備份基本上需要關機的 hello VM 透過 hello Azure 入口網站，並 hello 基底 VM 磁碟的複本及所有附加 Vhd toohello VM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1532">hello offline backup would basically require a shutdown of hello VM through hello Azure Portal and a copy of hello base VM disk plus all attached VHDs toohello VM.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1533">這會保留 hello VM 時間映像中的點和其相關聯的磁碟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1533">This would preserve a point in time image of hello VM and its associated disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1534">建議 toocopy hello 「 備份 」 到不同的 Azure 儲存體帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1534">It is recommended toocopy hello ‘backups’ into a different Azure Storage Account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1535">因此 hello 章節所述的程序[Azure 儲存體帳戶之間複製磁碟][ planning-guide-5.4.2]本文件將會套用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1535">Hence hello procedure described in chapter [Copying disks between Azure Storage Accounts][planning-guide-5.4.2] of this document would apply.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1536">除了 hello 關機使用 hello 其中一個 Azure 入口網站也可以執行它透過 Powershell 或 CLI 如下所述： <https://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/virtual-machines-deploy-rmtemplates-powershell/></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1536">Besides hello shutdown using hello Azure Portal one can also do it via Powershell or CLI as described here : <https://azure.microsoft.com/documentation/articles/virtual-machines-deploy-rmtemplates-powershell/></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1537">還原該狀態會組成刪除 hello、 基本 VM 與 hello 原始磁碟的 hello 基底 VM 及掛接的 Vhd 複製後的 hello 儲存 Vhd toohello 原始儲存體帳戶，然後重新部署 hello 系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1537">A restore of that state would consist of deleting hello base VM as well as hello original disks of hello base VM and mounted VHDs, copying back hello saved VHDs toohello original Storage Account and then redeploying hello system.</span></span>

### <a name="online-backup-of-an-sap-system"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1540">SAP 系統的線上備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1540">Online backup of an SAP system</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1541">在 hello 中所述以 DBMS 專用方法執行備份的 hello DBMS [DBMS 指南][dbms-guide]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1541">Backup of hello DBMS is performed with DBMS specific methods as described in hello [DBMS Guide][dbms-guide].</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1542">Hello SAP 系統內的其他 Vm 可以備份使用 Azure 虛擬機器備份功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1542">Other VMs within hello SAP system can be backed up using Azure Virtual Machine Backup functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1543">Azure 虛擬機器備份引進早期 2015年中，並同時是標準方法 toobackup 完成 VM 在 Azure 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1543">Azure Virtual Machine Backup got introduced early in 2015 and meanwhile is a standard method toobackup a complete VM in Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1544">Azure 備份儲存在 Azure 中的 hello 備份，並允許虛擬機器還原一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1544">Azure Backup stores hello backups in Azure and allows a restore of a VM again.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1545">自 2015 年 12 月使用 VM 備份不會保留 hello 唯一 VM 識別碼是用於 SAP 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1545">As of Dec 2015 using VM Backup does NOT keep hello unique VM ID which is used for SAP licensing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1546">這表示從 VM 備份進行還原，需要安裝新的 SAP 授權金鑰示為 hello 已還原的 VM 會被視為 toobe 新的 VM 和已儲存的先前一個取代。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1546">This means that a restore from a VM backup requires installation of a new SAP license key as hello restored VM is considered toobe a new VM and not a replacement of the former one which was saved.</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1547">截至 2016 年 1 月為止，Azure VM 備份目前尚未支援使用 Azure Resourc Manager 部署的 VM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1547">As of Jan 2016 Azure VM Backup doesn't support VMs that are deployed with Azure Resourc Manager yet.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1550">理論上執行的資料庫可以備份以一致的方式以及如果 hello DBMS 系統支援 hello Windows VSS 的 Vm (磁碟區陰影複製服務<https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/bb968832 (vs.85> ) 一樣例如 SQL Server。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1550">Theoretically VMs that run databases can be backed up in a consistent manner as well if hello DBMS systems supports hello Windows VSS (Volume Shadow Copy Service <https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/bb968832(v=vs.85).aspx> ) as e.g. SQL Server does.</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1551">不過請注意，您無法根據 Azure VM 備份還原時間點來還原資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1551">However, be aware that based on Azure VM backups point-in-time restores of databases are not possible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1552">因此，建議使用 DBMS 功能，而不是依賴 Azure VM 備份的資料庫的 tooperform 備份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1552">Therefore, the recommendation is tooperform backups of databases with DBMS functionality instead of relying on Azure VM Backup</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1558">沒有任何對等的 tooWindows VSS 在 Linux 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1558">There is no equivalent tooWindows VSS in Linux.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1559">因此，您只能進行檔案一致備份，而無法進行應用程式一致備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1559">Therefore only file-consistent backups are possible but not application-consistent backups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1560">hello SAP DBMS 備份應該使用 DBMS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1560">hello SAP DBMS backup should be done using DBMS functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1561">hello 檔案系統，其中包括 hello SAP 相關可以儲存資料，例如使用 tar 檔案解壓縮述此處： <http://help.sap.com/saphelp_nw70ehp2/helpdata/en/d3/c0da3ccbb04d35b186041ba6ac301f/content.htm></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1561">hello file system which includes hello SAP related data can be saved e.g. using tar as described here : <http://help.sap.com/saphelp_nw70ehp2/helpdata/en/d3/c0da3ccbb04d35b186041ba6ac301f/content.htm></span></span>

### <a name="azure-as-dr-site-for-production-sap-landscapes"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1562">Azure 作為 SAP 生產環境的 DR 網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1562">Azure as DR site for production SAP landscapes</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1563">Mid 2014，因為 HYPER-V、 系統中心和 Azure 延伸模組 toovarious 元件可讓 Azure 的 hello 使用量執行內部部署 HYPER-V 為基礎的 vm 與 DR 網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1563">Since Mid 2014, extensions toovarious components around Hyper-V, System Center and Azure enable hello usage of Azure as DR site for VMs running on-premises based on Hyper-V.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1564">詳述如何 toodeploy 此解決方案的部落格記載於此： <http://blogs.msdn.com/b/saponsqlserver/archive/2014/11/19/protecting-sap-solutions-with-azure-site-recovery.aspx></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1564">A blog detailing how toodeploy this solution is documented here: <http://blogs.msdn.com/b/saponsqlserver/archive/2014/11/19/protecting-sap-solutions-with-azure-site-recovery.aspx></span></span>

## <a name="summary"></a><span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1565">摘要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1565">Summary</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1566">hello 關鍵點的高可用性 Azure 中 SAP 系統如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1566">hello key points of High Availability for SAP systems in Azure are:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1567">在此時間點，hello SAP 單一失敗點無法保護完全 hello 相同方式與可在內部部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1567">At this point in time, hello SAP single point of failure cannot be secured exactly hello same way as it can be done in on-premises deployments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1568">hello 原因是沒有 hello 使用第 3 個合作對象軟體，共用磁碟叢集，無法尚未建置在 Azure 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1568">hello reason is that Shared Disk clusters can’t yet be built in Azure without hello use of 3rd party software.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1569">對於 hello DBMS 層，您會需要 toouse 不依賴共用的磁碟叢集技術的 DBMS 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1569">For hello DBMS layer you need toouse DBMS functionality that does not rely on shared disk cluster technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1570">詳細資料會記載於 hello [DBMS 指南][dbms-guide]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1570">Details are documented in hello [DBMS Guide][dbms-guide].</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1571">toominimize hello hello Azure 基礎結構或主機維護故障 」 網域內有問題的影響，您應該使用 Azure 可用性設定組：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1571">toominimize hello impact of problems within Fault Domains in hello Azure infrastructure or host maintenance, you should use Azure Availability Sets:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1572">建議一個 toohave hello SAP 應用程式層可用性設定組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1572">It is recommended toohave one Availability Set for hello SAP application layer.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1573">建議的 toohave hello SAP DBMS 層個別的可用性設定組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1573">It is recommended toohave a separate Availability Set for hello SAP DBMS layer.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1574">不建議 tooapply hello 相同可用性設定組不同 SAP 系統的 Vm。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1574">It is NOT recommended tooapply hello same Availability set for VMs of different SAP systems.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1575">為了備份 hello SAP DBMS 層，請檢查 hello [DBMS 指南][dbms-guide]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1575">For Backup purposes of hello SAP DBMS layer, please check hello [DBMS Guide][dbms-guide].</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1576">備份 SAP Dialog 執行個體就很少的有意義，因為它是通常更快的 tooredeploy 簡單的對話執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1576">Backing up SAP Dialog instances makes little sense since it is usually faster tooredeploy simple dialog instances.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1577">備份 hello VM 所在的 hello SAP 系統，並與其 hello 全域目錄 hello 不同執行個體的所有 hello 設定檔就很重要，應該使用 Windows 備份執行或例如 tar 檔案解壓縮在 Linux 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1577">Backing up hello VM which contains hello global directory of hello SAP system and with it all hello profiles of hello different instances, does make sense and should be performed with Windows Backup or e.g. tar on Linux.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f86b6-1578">由於 Windows Server 2008 (R2) 和 Windows Server 2012 (R2)，使其更容易 toobackup 之間有差異使用較新的 hello Windows Server 版本，我們建議 toorun 做為 Windows 客體作業系統的 Windows Server 2012 (R2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f86b6-1578">Since there are differences between Windows Server 2008 (R2) and Windows Server 2012 (R2), which make it easier toobackup using hello more recent Windows Server releases, we recommend toorun Windows Server 2012 (R2) as Windows guest operating system.</span></span>
